## BLAST RADIUS SUMMARY

**Every FastAPI route that uses dependencies** — which is effectively every route in a typical application — passes through `solve_dependencies`. The function is the **single choke point** for dependency injection in FastAPI.

```
solve_dependencies (utils.py:598-735)
 ├── recursive call for each sub-dependency (utils.py:649)
 ├── get_request_handler → all HTTP routes (routing.py:457)
 └── get_websocket_app → all WebSocket routes (routing.py:751)
```

- **Direct impact**: 2 callers in `fastapi/routing.py` + 1 self-call
- **Transitive impact**: Every `APIRouter`/`FastAPI` app route, every dependency graph traversal
- **Test coverage gap**: Zero direct unit tests. Entirely reliant on integration/routing tests
- **Cluster coupling**: Strong predicted coupling (19 edges) to response-class tests — a change that alters error shapes propagates there

---

## ACTIONABILITY CHECKLIST

| # | Action | Rationale | Urgency |
|---|--------|-----------|---------|
| 1 | Add direct unit tests for `solve_dependencies` **before** making any change | Zero direct test coverage currently exists — regression risk is maximally unmitigated | **HIGH** |
| 2 | Pin the `SolvedDependency` return type — do not change field names/types | Both `get_request_handler` and `get_websocket_app` destructure `.errors`, `.values`, `.dependency_updates` | **HIGH** |
| 3 | Run full `tests/` suite after any change | Integration coverage is the only safety net; 19-edge coupling to response-class tests means regressions may surface there | **HIGH** |
| 4 | Check `dependency_cache` key format if modifying cache behavior | Cache key (`DependencyCacheKey`) flows through recursive calls and into sub-dependency resolution | **MEDIUM** |
| 5 | Audit `async_exit_stack` lifecycle | Passed in from callers and used within the function for context-manager-based dependencies | **MEDIUM** |
| 6 | Verify WebSocket path separately if changing request-type-dependent logic | `get_websocket_app` passes `websocket` (a `WebSocket` instance) as `request` — behavior may diverge | **MEDIUM** |
| 7 | Review `embed_body_fields` parameter propagation | Only used in the HTTP handler path (routing.py), but the param exists in the function signature | **LOW** |
| 8 | Check release notes for prior behavioral changes at docs line 1179 and 2354 | Historical context may reveal why certain design decisions (e.g. no tests) were made | **LOW** |
